to Take Sleeping Pills","summary":"Theres a smart way to use sleep remedies, whether theyre the over-the-counter variety, or prescribed by your doctor.","body":"\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w539\u002F7a6ad6ba1bde022277df37247bf4fc04e55845ea.jpg\" alt=\"When to Take Sleeping Pills\" width=\"539\" height=\"810\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003E\u003Cb\u003EAre sleeping pills healthy or a bad alternative? \u003C\u002Fb\u003E(Photo Courtesy of Getty Images)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EIf you&#x2019;ve ever wondered about how safe popping a few sleeping pills can actually be, you&#x2019;re not alone: In the last few years, researchers have linked the drugs to higher instances of early death, Alzheimer&#x2019;s, increased mortality, and most recently, a doubled risk of car crashes. Such facts make it tough to tell whether you should risk your health for a decent night&#x2019;s sleep. According to sleep specialists and neurologists, there&#x2019;s a smart way to use sleep remedies, whether they&#x2019;re the over-the-counter variety, or prescribed by your doctor. And while natural remedies will usually&#xA0;trump chemical concoctions, you can safely use these drugs as long as you follow a few guidelines, know your body, and understand their biggest risks.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated:\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.mensjournal.com\u002Fexpert-advice\u002F9-ways-lack-of-sleep-is-killing-you-20140416?utm_source=yahoohealth&amp;utm_medium=referral&amp;utm_campaign=sleepingpills\"\u003E\u003Ci\u003E 9 Ways Lack of Sleep Is Killing You\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E \u003Cb\u003EOnly when you absolutely have to.\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"790\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002Fe6ec3b9f7ab1b6a93c4ee1f2fe544fb2b9668e1e.jpg\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003E(Photo Courtesy of Getty Images)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EThe safest and healthiest way to use sleeping pills is &#x201C;to avoid them as much as possible unless absolutely needed,&#x201D; says Dr. Mark Boulos, a neurologist at Toronto&#x2019;s Sunnybrook Health Science, citing &#x201C;the night before you go in for surgery, or for only a few days at a time during stressful times in life&#x201D; as good examples. Columbia neurology professor Dr. Carl Bazil adds that before going in for any pill treatment either at the pharmacy or with your doctor, first take a look at your sleeping habits since these could be the roots of your problem. &#x201C;People don&#x2019;t often think about it, but stimulants late in the day like caffeine, chocolate, or nicotine keep people awake,&#x201D; he says. Then there&#x2019;s your smartphone or tablet, whose light tends to trick your body into thinking it isn&#x2019;t bedtime yet. &#x201C;If you&#x2019;re working up to the time you go to bed, you won&#x2019;t be able to just turn it off,&#x201D; Bazil says. &#x201C;You need time to lie down and let your brain relax.&#x201D; If you&#x2019;ve checked your habits and you&#x2019;re still having trouble sleeping, that&#x2019;s when you should consider a pill.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated: \u003Ci\u003E1\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.mensjournal.com\u002Fexpert-advice\u002F10-common-bad-habits-and-how-to-break-them-20150108?utm_source=yahoohealth&amp;utm_medium=referral&amp;utm_campaign=sleepingpills\"\u003E0 Common Bad Habits and How to Break Them\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E \u003Cb\u003EAfter reading the ingredients.\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"405\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F96e3d8119329dcc0ac1c21362cc742652b03dbf3.jpg\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003E(Photo Courtesy of Getty Images)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EBoth over-the-counter and prescription pills can be dangerous if used in high doses, so it&#x2019;s all about using the drugs properly, says Boulos. Bazil adds you can start with over the counter medicines, but know what&#x2019;s in your pills, first. The most popular pharmacy-available medicines contain antihistamine &#x2014; the main ingredient that makes you drowsy. &#x201C;The main problem with antihistamines in many OTC sleep remedies is they last too long,&#x201D; says Bazil. &#x201C;So you still have to be aware that you could still be drowsy the next day from the medicine, not from lack of sleep.&#x201D; Other OTC drugs have melatonin, a hormone, which helps re-train and set your body clock if you&#x2019;re trying to regulate your sleeping time. You can also opt for herbal remedies, like Valerian, or supplements with amino acids. But keep in mind there are several signs you should see a doctor, Bazil says. If your sleep troubles are persistent, you get enough sleep but still feel sleepy, or if you wake up frequently, or with headaches, you could have a disorder.\u003Cbr\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003Cb\u003EYou have enough time for them.\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"415\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F65f722715ea83f5f4fea341dd88700be6ca950fc.jpg\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003E(Photo Courtesy of Getty Images)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ESleeping pills, by definition, mess with your body&#x2019;s natural behavior (their biggest effects include sedation, slurred speech, and uncoordinated actions) so be extra cautious of when you take them &#x2014;&#xA0;and make no plans to do anything important but sleep for that block of time. &#x201C;Remember these [pills] are meant to make you drowsy, and some of them have the tendency to make you forget things,&#x201D; says Bazil. &#x201C;That&#x2019;s all fine if you go to sleep, but some people won&#x2019;t feel sleepy, so they&#x2019;ll decide to take it, and wait until they do feel drowsy.&#x201D; The problem is, the sedative&#x2019;s effects can hit you quickly at unexpected times, like while driving. &#x201C;All of a sudden you&#x2019;re half asleep, which can result in confused or dangerous behavior,&#x201D; Bazil says. A&#xA0;\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Farchpsyc.jamanetwork.com\u002Farticle.aspx?articleid=1885708\"\u003E2014 CDC report\u003C\u002Fa\u003E&#xA0;found that a high number of emergency room visits were caused by adverse reactions to Ambien, the most popular prescription insomnia-aid &#x2013; and they included a high number of falls, confused behavior, and difficulty waking up. The&#xA0;\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.fda.gov\u002FDrugs\u002FDrugSafety\u002Fucm334041.htm\"\u003EFDA also warns\u003C\u002Fa\u003E&#xA0;about &#x201C;next-morning impairment&#x201D;, or when the drug&#x2019;s effects last longer than you&#x2019;d think. Bazil says since sleeping pills are long acting, even when you wake up, there&#x2019;s a possibility that you&#x2019;re still in a confused state and not 100 percent alert. The lesson is simple: Always follow the recommended dose, and take sleeping pills right before you hit the sack, allowing extra time for any lingering after-effects.\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated: \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.mensjournal.com\u002Fexpert-advice\u002F10-products-to-help-you-get-a-better-nights-sleep-20140310?utm_source=yahoohealth&amp;utm_medium=referral&amp;utm_campaign=sleepingpills\"\u003E\u003Ci\u003E10 Products to Help You Get a Better Night&#x2019;s Sleep\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E \u003Cb\u003EIf you&#x2019;re not already hooked.\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"361\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002Fe112e22e08987ddbc01c5aba53715ebbae0bdfd2.jpg\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003E(Photo Courtesy of Getty Images)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ENot all sleeping pills are made equal (Ambien is thought to be less addictive in its ingredients than benzodiazepines like Xanax) but treat all with caution: Whatever you&#x2019;re taking, your body still adapts and becomes immune to sleeping pills fast &#x2014;&#xA0;neutralizing their effect and often tricking you into thinking you need a higher dosage. &#x201C;With on-going use, [the drug&#x2019;s] effectiveness wears off,&#x201D; Boulos says. &#x201C;At this point, the user needs to increase the dose and then it turns into a vicious cycle &#x2014;&#xA0;increased dose, effect of medication wears off, increased dose again and so on.&#x201D; You&#x2019;ll know when you&#x2019;ve used sleeping pills too much when their effectiveness starts to wear off, Boulos says, so avoid daily or regular use so you don&#x2019;t reach that point.\u003Cb\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated:\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.mensjournal.com\u002Fexpert-advice\u002F8-most-addictive-legal-drugs-20140226?utm_source=yahoohealth&amp;utm_medium=referral&amp;utm_campaign=sleepingpills\"\u003E \u003Ci\u003E8 Most Addictive Legal Drugs\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E \u003Cb\u003EWhen you&#x2019;re sober and off other medications\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"360\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F4ca85a31d985090db73a707f2b54344ac275cac6.jpg\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003E(Photo Courtesy of Getty Images)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E&#x201C;The biggest danger associated with sleeping pills is if they are overdosed or mixed with alcohol or another sedating medication,&#x201D; says Boulos. &#x201C;This can be deadly, as has been the case with several celebrities over the past few years.&#x201D; That&#x2019;s because alcohol, a depressant, intensifies the sedative, drowsy effect of sleeping pills &#x2014;&#xA0;putting you at a bigger risk for injuries resulting from confused behavior. Read the label on your medicine: Don&#x2019;t drink within 24 hours of taking a pill and check with your pharmacist or doctor about any current medications you&#x2019;re taking before starting a new treatment.\u003Cbr\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003Cb\u003EAfter fully assessing your sleep habits.\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"764\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F62b60a2f4e3da45a40592b3e3d04eed1e9c8dec3.jpg\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003E(Photo Courtesy of Getty Images)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EThe sleeping pill shouldn&#x2019;t be your cop-out for bad sleep behavior. According to Bazil, it&#x2019;s easy to believe that if you take a sleeping pill, you can still have terrible sleeping habits, including working up until the last minute at night or leaving your phone on. &#x201C;They&#x2019;ll expect the pill to overcome all those problems, or make up for not sleeping enough,&#x201D; says Bazil. &#x201C;It won&#x2019;t. You still need to pay attention to your body to prepare yourself for sleep, and give adequate time for it.&#x201D;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated: \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.mensjournal.com\u002Fexpert-advice\u002Fsigns-you-might-have-a-sleep-disorder-20150504?utm_source=yahoohealth&amp;utm_medium=referral&amp;utm_campaign=sleepingpills\"\u003E\u003Ci\u003ESigns You Might Have a Sleep Disorder\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003Cb\u003EThe natural remedies don&#x2019;t work.\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"304\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002Fb91a7c91ad61ebf50401de4af598d15c7e2e7901.jpg\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003E9Photo Courtesy of Getty Images0\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EA whole host of new studies show that natural alternatives like&#xA0;\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.mensjournal.com\u002Fhealth-fitness\u002Fhealth\u002Fhow-meditation-can-help-you-sleep-better-20150225\"\u003Emindfulness meditation\u003C\u002Fa\u003E&#xA0;and even&#xA0;\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.mensjournal.com\u002Fhealth-fitness\u002Fhealth\u002Fa-diet-to-help-get-your-sleep-back-on-track-20140718\"\u003Echanging your dinner diet\u003C\u002Fa\u003E&#xA0;can help you get to sleep easier. In a recent&#xA0;\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fannals.org\u002Farticle.aspx?articleid=2301405\"\u003Emeta-analysis of 20 studies\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, researchers found that cognitive behavioral therapy worked very similar to&#xA0;medicine for people with insomnia, but without the sedated side effects. You could also make some personal time to de-stress: Boulos recommends doing a relaxing activity before bedtime, like a massage with your significant other, or having a warm shower.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003EBy Jillian Rose Lim \u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003Cb\u003EMore From Men&#x2019;s Things That Make You Lose Your Voice","summary":"I havent had a cold in months, but I keep losing my voice.","body":"\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002Fd92819b26b5fdcce558afbf8268ac4431d447a7c.jpg\" alt=\"4 Things That Make You Lose Your Voice\" width=\"540\" height=\"279\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003E\u003Cb\u003EI haven&#x2019;t had a cold in months, but I keep losing my voice. What&#x2019;s going on? \u003C\u002Fb\u003E(\u003Ci\u003EPhoto: Getty Images)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ELaryngitis (the most common cause of hoarseness or voice loss) happens when your voice box becomes irritated or inflamed, leading to swelling that keeps your vocal cords from being able to open and close smoothly. (This vocal cord movement is what creates sound.) A viral infection, like a cold or the flu, is the usual culprit, but it&#x2019;s not the only one.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EStrain is also a top cause of laryngitis; just one night of cheering at a sporting event or concert can bring it on. Voice strain should go away on its own with rest and lots of fluids. But you really have to rest your voice, especially if you&#x2019;ve lost it entirely: Not only will staying quiet help you heal faster, but taxing your voice during laryngitis can damage vocal cords further and can lead to the formation of polyps or nodules that may require surgery.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated:\u003C\u002Fb\u003E \u003Ci\u003E\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.health.com\u002Fhealth\u002Fgallery\u002F0,,20640098,00.html?xid=yahoo-voice-070615\"\u003E\u003Cb\u003E10 Ways to Soothe a Sore Throat\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EIf hoarseness persists beyond a few weeks or keeps coming back, there may be something else going on. One possibility is acid reflux. When stomach acid comes back up the esophagus, it can cause irritation of the vocal cords. The type of reflux most associated with voice issues is called laryngopharyngeal reflux disease, and it often doesn&#x2019;t cause heartburn or nausea. Your doctor can prescribe antacids and other medication (like steroids) that can help your voice if it&#x2019;s not getting better.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EAnother possible cause is a yeast infection in your throat, also called oral thrush. This appears most often in people with depressed immune systems, like those with HIV or cancer, but people using a corticosteroid inhaler to treat their asthma are also more prone. That&#x2019;s because the steroid can locally decrease your immune function, which allows the overgrowth of yeast. Oral antifungals can solve it.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated: \u003Ci\u003E\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.health.com\u002Fhealth\u002Fgallery\u002F0,,20529772,00.html?xid=yahoo-voice-070615\"\u003E11 Surprising Symptoms of Acid Reflux\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ETo get a diagnosis, see an ear, nose and throat specialist (ENT), who can take a look at your vocal cords with a scope to determine if acid reflux or yeast is robbing you of your voice. An ENT can also rule out something more serious, like laryngeal cancer, which often occurs with ear pain and a sore throat on top of voice issues.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003EHealth&#x2018;s medical editor, Roshini Rajapaksa, MD, is assistant professor of medicine at the NYU School of Medicine and co-founder of Tula Skincare.\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003EMore from Health.com:\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ca Symptoms\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.health.com\u002Fhealth\u002Fgallery\u002F0,,20834752,00.html?xid=yahoo-voice-070615\"\u003E\u003Cb\u003E15 Diseases Doctors Misdiagnose\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ca 02FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F7655b2069eac79eb9a7651baf8945fb7e277b68e.jpg","type":"image\u002Fjpeg","width":540,"height":359,"size_type":"original","formats":{}}],"url":"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002Foriginal\u002FHuTjk9dlsUkdEtSTnXW3GmC4lXk","source_url":"http:\u002F\u002F41.media.tumblr.com\u002F2b0f8e77ad9637f061592be74590ae86\u002Ftumblr_inline_nr8tp1WqGQ1sdn8q2_540.jpg"}],"highlight_color":"#000000","data_version":"1","title":"I Spent Thousands to Keep My Sick Cat Alive. I Dont Think Id Do It Again.","summary":"Even as I said it, I knew it was ridiculous and selfish. Just promise youll make it till my 30th birthday.","body":"\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F7655b2069eac79eb9a7651baf8945fb7e277b68e.jpg\" alt=\"I Spent Thousands to Keep My Sick Cat Alive. I Don&#x2019;t Think I&#x2019;d Do It Again.\" width=\"540\" height=\"359\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003E\u003Cb\u003EWhen it comes to pet health costs, is it worth it?&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fb\u003E(Photo: Makovsvet\u002FGetty Images)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EEven as I said it, I knew it was ridiculous and selfish. &#x201C;Just promise you&#x2019;ll make it till my 30th birthday,&#x201D; I said quietly to Kitty, my tiny ten-year-old cat. We were both underneath my bed, where she&#x2019;d decamped the minute we returned home from a long day at the vet. Earlier that day, she&#x2019;d been diagnosed with a terminal heart condition. Nearly two and a half years later, she&#x2019;d die from it, in a cold and unfamiliar emergency room in the middle of the night.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated:\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fnymag.com\u002Fscienceofus\u002F2015\u002F01\u002Fokay-to-be-an-overbearing-pet-parent.html?mid=yahoohealth\"\u003E\u003Ci\u003E It&#x2019;s Okay to Be an Overbearing Pet Parent\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EThis was a longer prognosis than any vet predicted, and yet, in the months since her death, I can&#x2019;t stop wondering whether I did the right thing in delaying the inevitable for so long. The twice-a-day pills, the bimonthly visits to the veterinary cardiologist (which almost always included a chest tap, a risky, invasive procedure that drained fluid from in and around her lungs), not to mention the vast sums of money spent on it all: Were these things really for her, or were they mostly, selfishly, for me? Saying good-bye to a pet has never been easy, but advances in modern veterinary care can make it near-impossible for pet owners to know when to let go. It&#x2019;s an ethical quandary that&#x2019;s in some ways unsettlingly similar \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fnymag.com\u002Fscienceofus\u002F2014\u002F10\u002Fatul-gawande-on-being-mortal.html?mid=yahoohealth\"\u003Eto aging and end-of-life issues currently plaguing human medicine\u003C\u002Fa\u003E: Just because we can extend a life, should we?\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EOnce, the biggest moral dilemma veterinarians faced was that pet owners were hasty and thoughtless in their decision to euthanize, requesting the procedure at the first sign of age, illness, or mere inconvenience. Now it&#x2019;s often the opposite extreme, said Bernard Rollin, a professor of philosophy and animal sciences at Colorado State University, who in 2011 wrote a\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov\u002Fpubmed\u002F21601753\"\u003E paper\u003C\u002Fa\u003E for the journal \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.elsevier.com\u002Fjournals\u002Fveterinary-clinics-of-north-america-small-animal-practice\u002F0195-5616\"\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003Ca\u003EVeterinary Clinics of North America\u003C\u002Fa\u003E: Small Practice about the stress this causes veterinarians. &#x201C;In a major ironic twist of fate, rather than human medicine learning the wisdom of euthanasia for suffering animals from veterinary medicine &#x2026; veterinary medicine assimilated some of the more pernicious aspects of human medicine,&#x201D; Rollin wrote. &#x201C;In particular, as animals became increasingly viewed as members of the family, the reluctance to euthanize began to enter veterinary medicine.&#x201D;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EA pet is not a person, and the end-of-life decisions for each are not the same. As science writer Carl Safina explains the distinction in his forthcoming\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.amazon.com\u002FBeyond-Words-What-Animals-Think\u002Fdp\u002F0805098887\"\u003E book\u003C\u002Fa\u003E Beyond Words: What Animals Think and Feel, &#x201C;I don&#x2019;t mean to imply that I value the life of a fish or a bird the same way I value a human life, but their presence in the world has as much validity as does our presence.&#x201D; It&#x2019;s not the same, but each life still has value in its own way.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated: \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fnymag.com\u002Fscienceofus\u002F2015\u002F01\u002Fhow-pets-help-kids-with-autism.html?mid=yahoohealth\"\u003E\u003Ci\u003EHow Pets Help Kids With Autism\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EAnd Rollin is right about the pets-as-family idea. A 2013\u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.avma.org\u002FKB\u002FResources\u002FStatistics\u002FPages\u002FMarket-research-statistics-US-Pet-Ownership-Demographics-Sourcebook.aspx\"\u003E survey\u003C\u002Fa\u003E by the American Veterinary Medical Association found that two thirds of dog owners consider the animal part of their family, up from just over half in a 2006 survey. (The numbers are lower for cats, but they also show an upward trend.) &#x201C;The human-animal bond has grown &#x2014; it&#x2019;s accepted, it&#x2019;s recognized, I think, at least in part because of the change of social structure in families,&#x201D; said Jane Shaw, a professor of veterinary medicine at Colorado State University. She&#x2019;s referring to the rise in \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.nbcnews.com\u002Fhealth\u002Fhealth-news\u002Fnew-normal-cohabitation-rise-study-finds-f1C9208429\"\u003Ecohabitation\u003C\u002Fa\u003E and \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.pewsocialtrends.org\u002F2010\u002F06\u002F25\u002Fchildlessness-up-among-all-women-down-among-women-with-advanced-degrees\u002F\"\u003Echildlessness\u003C\u002Fa\u003E among Americans, or of the increased number of those who are putting \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Ftwentysomethingmarriage.org\u002F\"\u003Emarriage off\u003C\u002Fa\u003E or never \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.pewsocialtrends.org\u002F2014\u002F09\u002F24\u002Frecord-share-of-americans-have-never-married\u002F\"\u003Egetting around to it at all\u003C\u002Fa\u003E. There are more ways to form families these days, and, as a result, &#x201C;pets are filling a big role for many people,&#x201D; Shaw said. &#x201C;And it means many people are willing to invest the same level of care for their animals as they are for human families.&#x201D;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EAmericans spent $56 billion on their pets in 2013, according to the latest figures from the Federal Trade Commission; of that, $7.6 billion went to prescription and over-the-counter drugs for cats and dogs. That&#x2019;s\u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.ftc.gov\u002Fsystem\u002Ffiles\u002Fdocuments\u002Freports\u002Fcompetition-pet-medications-industry-prescription-portability-distribution-practices\u002F150526-pet-meds-report.pdf\"\u003E expected\u003C\u002Fa\u003E to grow to $10.2 billion annually by 2018. Indeed, many pet owners are willing to shell out substantial amounts of money on veterinary care: In a 2010\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fsurveys.ap.org\u002Fdata%5CGfK%5CAP-GfK%20Petside%20Topline%20for%20final%20060710_4th%20release.pdf\"\u003E survey\u003C\u002Fa\u003E of more than a thousand pet owners, 42 percent said they&#x2019;d be somewhat to very likely to spend $5,000 on a single treatment for their pets. Tara Parker-Pope of the New York Times\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwell.blogs.nytimes.com\u002F2010\u002F06\u002F09\u002Fhow-much-would-you-spend-on-a-sick-pet\u002F?_r=0\"\u003E noted\u003C\u002Fa\u003E that the pet owner&#x2019;s annual income did not make a difference in their answers &#x2014; those earning $50,000 per year answered similarly to those earning more.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EBut the cost of treatment for a slow-acting illness like Kitty&#x2019;s was deceptively exorbitant. I could never agree to pay $5,000 in one go, but $300 here, $75 there? The smaller costs added up. By the end, I was spending about $150 per month on medication and $300 to $800 every other month on visits to a specialist; once, I paid more than $2,000 for an overnight stay in a\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.veterinaryspecialtycare.com\u002Fsurgical-careChamber.php?1\"\u003E hyperbaric oxygen chamber\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, to help her breathing return to normal. I felt equal parts panicky over the expenses and guilty over my mounting financial anxiety, and I noticed that when discussing treatment, the question never seemed to be what was best in the long run for Kitty (or for me, for that matter).\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated: \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fnymag.com\u002Fscienceofus\u002F2014\u002F07\u002Fdogs-can-get-jealous-suggests-adorable-study.html?mid=yahoohealth\"\u003E\u003Ci\u003EDogs Can Get Jealous, Suggests Adorable Study\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ENot so long ago, even if you&#x2019;d wanted to drop thousands on a pet&#x2019;s medical care, it wasn&#x2019;t an option. Eleven years ago, Cornell \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.vet.cornell.edu\u002Fnews\u002Farticles\u002Fmri.htm\"\u003Edeveloped\u003C\u002Fa\u003E the first MRI machine designed for pets. Six years ago, some vets began \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.usatoday.com\u002Fstory\u002Fnews\u002Fnation\u002F2014\u002F02\u002F05\u002Fpets-stem-cell-treatment\u002F5224363\u002F\"\u003Eoffering \u003C\u002Fa\u003Estem-cell therapy for dogs, to ease the symptoms of chronic illnesses like arthritis. In many respects, advances like these are a wonderful thing, both for the animals and the people who love them. Initially for Kitty, a chest tap would buy her several solid months of easier breathing, so her vets and I decided the temporary discomfort of the 20-or-so-minute procedure was worth the cost (financial for me, psychic for &#x2014; well, for both of us). They warned me that a time would come when she&#x2019;d need them much more frequently, and the risk and distress would outweigh the benefits. But for the moment, they assured, things were okay. I focused on the moment.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EIf I&#x2019;m ever in this situation again, though, I&#x2019;ll look farther ahead. As it stands now, Americans have the chance to ensure that their pets get the planned, peaceful exits out of this world that their human loved ones \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fnymag.com\u002Fdaily\u002Fintelligencer\u002F2014\u002F11\u002Fdeath-with-dignity-backer-brittany-maynard-dies.html?mid=yahoohealth\"\u003Eoften do not\u003C\u002Fa\u003E. &#x201C;In the end, you have to make a judgment, one that we&#x2019;re socially not in a position where we make it for ourselves or for our relatives,&#x201D; Rollin said. &#x201C;But you are forced to make it for the animal. I like to think of death as a closing to a life. &#x2026; And you don&#x2019;t want the animal to close on its life in misery.&#x201D; In hindsight, I can see the point I should&#x2019;ve shifted course to planning a good death for Kitty rather than stubbornly fighting for her life. Last summer, the chest taps started increasing in frequency &#x2014; once, she needed three in a month. &#x201C;These are not benign and have the potential to cause bleeding,&#x201D; the emergency vet wrote in the medical records after the third one, adding that each tap created inflammation and scar tissue. And yet her vets and I decided to stay the course; even as the taps increased to every other month, the cardiologist (whom I liked very much) and I never spoke of prepping for the end of her life.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EBut then, even veterinarians struggle with these decisions. Rollin believes he hung on too long to a German shepherd he once had; the dog developed a degenerative spinal disease, and after a while, it couldn&#x2019;t walk. &#x201C;I&#x2019;d come home six, seven times a day and move him, so he didn&#x2019;t get bedsores,&#x201D; Rollin said. &#x201C;I think now: Was that the right thing to do? I think, now, that I waited too long.&#x201D;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated: \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fnymag.com\u002Fthecut\u002F2014\u002F12\u002Fcelebrity-pets-with-big-personalities.html?mid=yahoohealth\"\u003E\u003Ci\u003E33 Celebrity Pets With Big Personalities\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EIt&#x2019;s so hard to know, in part because veterinary end-of-life care comes with complications that don&#x2019;t apply to human medicine. For one, with animals, there is the tiny matter that the patient can&#x2019;t speak. For another, pets can&#x2019;t comprehend the trade-off they&#x2019;re making in enduring the pain and terror of medical treatment now for the promise of more time later. &#x201C;All they know is, This hurts now,&#x201D; Rollin told me. &#x201C;And they look up at you, and they want you to make it stop. And if you&#x2019;re doing it for eight months to garner another three months &#x2014; you see what I mean? I don&#x2019;t think that&#x2019;s fair to the animal. The animal doesn&#x2019;t know anything about the last three months. It&#x2019;s just miserable. And thank God, really, we&#x2019;re in a position to give them a decent death.&#x201D; For some pet owners, a decent death means turning\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fpetrequiem.com\u002Fabout-us\u002F\"\u003E to pet hospice\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, or in-home euthanasia; for others, it&#x2019;s a conversation with their regular vet about making the decision to euthanize before an emergency situation forces it. In either case, it takes an enormous amount of unselfish courage to recognize when it&#x2019;s best for the animal to let them go.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EIn Atul Gawande&#x2019;s 2014 book\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fnymag.com\u002Fscienceofus\u002F2014\u002F10\u002Fatul-gawande-on-being-mortal.html?mid=yahoohealth\"\u003E Being Mortal\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, he talks about how to make the final years of life meaningful for the aged and the ill. Before your loved one gets truly incapacitated in sickness, Gawande suggests clarifying what, exactly, makes life worth living for them. One man&#x2019;s list, memorably recounted in the book, was very short: ice cream and college football. As long as he&#x2019;s well and alert enough to eat his favorite food and watch his favorite football team, he&#x2019;s happy. Again: Pets are not people. But the lesson here applies. &#x201C;When the animal gets very sick, particularly with a terminal disease like cancer,&#x201D; Rollin said. &#x201C;you consult that list, and you make sure your own needs, your own guilt, are not prolonging the animal&#x2019;s suffering.&#x201D;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EI know what Kitty&#x2019;s would have included: Watching East 73rd Street from the bedroom window, something she did with such intense focus my boyfriend Andrew and I called it Cat TV. Jumping on top of one of us when we went to bed, to sleep perched on one of our backs or sides. Wolfing down the can of Fancy Feast before I barely had the chance to dump it in her bowl. I said earlier that pets can&#x2019;t speak, but, then &#x2014; that&#x2019;s not entirely true, is it? They can&#x2019;t literally talk, but\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fnymag.com\u002Fscienceofus\u002F2015\u002F04\u002Fyour-cat-is-trying-to-talk-to-you.html\"\u003E they can and do communicate\u003C\u002Fa\u003E. And when they stop doing the things they&#x2019;ve always loved, they&#x2019;re telling us they&#x2019;re getting ready to go.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated: \u003Ci\u003E\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fnymag.com\u002Fscienceofus\u002F2015\u002F04\u002Fyour-cat-is-trying-to-talk-to-you.html?mid=yahoohealth\"\u003EYour Cat Is Trying to Talk to You\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EMy 30th came and went, and with it the (unfair and silly, not to mention one-sided) &#x201C;agreement&#x201D; I&#x2019;d made with Kitty. I don&#x2019;t know if her health truly unraveled in the weeks after that, or if it was that I finally forced myself to look at it squarely. Probably, it was a little of both. One night, she didn&#x2019;t hop up on the bed with us. Later, I tried and failed to recall the last time I&#x2019;d seen her unwind with some Cat TV. The weekend before her death, she hardly touched her food, even the fanciest of Fancy Feast varietals. The following Monday, she tried to walk toward me but collapsed on her side halfway there, and I couldn&#x2019;t deny it any longer. I gently placed her in her carrier and headed with my boyfriend to the emergency vet for the last time.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EThere, the on-duty vet suggested we place her once again in a hyperbaric oxygen chamber, this time for several days. It wasn&#x2019;t guaranteed to help, and would bring the charges to at least $3,000. If we took her home, however, she&#x2019;d almost certainly die, painfully, and within hours. (These were the options laid out for us &#x2014; even then, no explicit mention of euthanasia.) Andrew and I asked for time to talk it over, and when the vet left us in the examination room, he (inadvertently, I assume) left the screen up that showed Kitty&#x2019;s medical records, and we saw the alarming frequency at which she&#x2019;d needed chest taps in recent months. We&#x2019;d already asked so much of her; the vast financial and emotional cost suddenly seemed too great to justify. We knew what we had to do, though even still I made a last attempt to hang on. (&#x201C;You can haunt us if you want!&#x201D; I blurted through my tears, stupidly.)\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EBefore the vet gave her the initial sedative, which preceded the injection to stop her failing heart, Kitty swiveled her head wildly around the exam room, taking in the grim metal surfaces with wide eyes. I hated that her last moments were spent in such a scary and strange environment, but it was too late to plan for a peaceful good-bye. She had been a very good kitty, and we told her so, as we each stroked her fur. Finally, I let her go.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003EBy \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fnymag.com\u002Fauthor\u002FMelissa%20Dahl\u002F\"\u003EMelissa Us\u003C\u002Fa\u003E:\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fnymag.com\u002Fscienceofus\u002F2015\u002F06\u002Fscience-of-us-animation-sleep-foot.html?mid=yahoohealth\"\u003EHow Your Feet Can Help You L&#xA0;\u003Ci\u003EChinsee)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EWhen it comes to dishing out sage relationship advice to our friends, you could practically call us Plato. But take that awesome-if-not-blunt advice ourselves? Not so much. Here are six pearls of wisdom we&#x2019;ve given out plenty of times but (come to think of it) don&#x2019;t actually heed in our own lives.\u003Ci\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E1. &#x201C;Just tell him how you feel.\u003C\u002Fb\u003E&#x201D; Whether you dig a new guy or you&#x2019;ve fallen head-over-heels for your longtime main man, it&#x2019;s often difficult to spit out your feelings to his face. More often than not, you&#x2019;ll find us egging on our friends, encouraging them to shake off their nerves, move past their fear of rejection, and let the love flow. But the second we&#x2019;re the one in the hot seat, we often clam up and have trouble sharing our feelings.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E2. &#x201C;Don&#x2019;t worry about it.\u003C\u002Fb\u003E&#x201D; When a first date hasn&#x2019;t texted for two days or you&#x2019;re willing to bet he&#x2019;ll forget your second anniversary&#x2014;in other words, in any relationship situation you can&#x2019;t control&#x2014;the only reasonable thing to do is let it go. And while we urge our friends to focus on \u003Ci\u003Eanything\u003C\u002Fi\u003E other than what&#x2019;s causing them worry, we ourselves get lost in Compulsive Thought Land \u003Ci\u003Emany\u003C\u002Fi\u003E times.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated: \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.glamour.com\u002Fsex-love-life\u002Fblogs\u002Fsmitten\u002F2015\u002F06\u002Fsigns-he-is-in-love-men-boyfriend?mbid=synd_yhealth\"\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Ci\u003E25 Unmistakable Signs He&#x2019;s in Love With You\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E3. &#x201C;Overanalyzing his cryptic text will get you nowhere.&#x201D; \u003C\u002Fb\u003EWhat did he mean by his simple &#x201C;sure?&#x201D; Maybe he meant he would rather do anything than attend the ballet by your side&#x2014;or maybe he just meant &#x201C;sure.&#x201D; We&#x2019;d tell a friend to put her sleuthing skills to better use by snagging a fabulous date-night dress on sale, but we&#x2019;d be staring nonstop at our phones trying to decipher the hidden meaning in that four-letter word.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E4. &#x201C;Don&#x2019;t text your ex.&#x201D;\u003C\u002Fb\u003E Don&#x2019;t text him to rub in your new relationship, don&#x2019;t text him sober and lonely&#x2014;and \u003Ci\u003Eno matter what,\u003C\u002Fi\u003E don&#x2019;t text him while drunk. Texting an ex only leads to more heartache, period. And yet, when we&#x2019;re missing a man we once loved, it&#x2019;s not always easy to stop before hitting Send.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated: \u003Cb\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.glamour.com\u002Fsex-love-life\u002F2008\u002F09\u002F10-things-hes-thinking-when-youre-naked?mbid=synd_yhealth\"\u003E\u003Ci\u003E10 Things He&#x2019;s Thinking When You&#x2019;re Naked\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E5. &#x201C;Snooping is never a good idea.&#x201D; \u003C\u002Fb\u003EIf you find nothing, we tell our friends, you&#x2019;ll feel guilty. And if you find something, how are you going to tell him? The act of snooping is wrong, but the need to know is strong&#x2014;much stronger than our own ability to resist sneaking a look at his vibrating phone when he leaves the room.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E6. &#x201C;Go out with Mr. Nice Guy.&#x201D; \u003C\u002Fb\u003EHe may not have serious sex appeal or arrive to pick you up on a motorcycle, but you can count on Mr. Nice Guy to come through in the ways that really matter. Mr. Nice Guy, we advise, is the man you marry. But when we&#x2019;re being asked on date number three by a perfectly nice guy we&#x2019;re just not attracted to, do we make up a reason to say no? You bet we do.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003EBy Jillian Kramer\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003EMore from Images)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EThat backyard BBQ party (okay, and the carafe of \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.self.com\u002Ffood\u002Frecipes\u002F2015\u002F07\u002Fhealthy-cocktails-summer-drinks-slideshow\u002F?mbid=synd_yhealth\"\u003Espiked lemonade\u003C\u002Fa\u003E) is calling your name, so let&#x2019;s get right to it. This brilliant upper body move&#x2014;called The Elbow Fly&#x2014;is from the team at The Barre Code and doesn&#x2019;t require any equipment. &#x201C;The exercise is great for your shoulders, upper and middle back and your chest,&#x201D; co-founders Ariana Chernin and Jillian Lorenz told us. Here&#x2019;s how to do it:\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" width=\"540\" height=\"341\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F2390878ad559935da442a6c5a6167649e409b07b.jpg\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003E(Photo: Courtesy of The Barre Code)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EStart standing with your feet directly under your hips and a slight bend in the knees. Bring your hands behind your head with your elbows wide. Squeeze your chest muscles and bring your elbows to meet in the middle of your torso without removing your hands from behind your head. Don&#x2019;t allow your elbows to dip below shoulder-height! Slowly reverse the movement (imagine you&#x2019;re trying to bring your shoulder blades to touch) to return to start. Do 25 reps.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EEasy, right? Finger Length May Say About Your Mental Health","summary":"Scientists in Turkey found that the length of a mans finger may predict his risk for schizophrenia.","body":"\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002Fe8411627ddc6a4659d0fd07f3371ab69be3ad4ac.jpg\" alt=\"What Finger Length May Say About Your Mental Health\" width=\"540\" height=\"303\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003E\u003Cb\u003ELook down at your hands, you&#x2019;d be surprised what you can learn about your brain.&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fb\u003E(Photo: Ian Andrews\u002FAlamy) &#xA0; &#xA0; &#xA0; &#xA0; &#xA0;\u003C\u002Fi\u003E&#xA0; \u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EIf your eyes are the windows to your soul, can your hands offer a peek into your mind? Possibly so, according to a recent study.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EScientists in Turkey found that the length of a man&#x2019;s finger &#x2014; particularly the ratio between his index and ring fingers &#x2014; may predict his risk for \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.everydayhealth.com\u002Femotional-health\u002Fschizophrenia\u002Findex.aspx?xid=y_sh\"\u003Eschizophrenia\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, a chronic, debilitating mental disorder characterized by hallucinations, delusions, and disordered thinking and behavior.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EBetween 2012 and 2013, the researchers measured the fingers of 103 \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.everydayhealth.com\u002Fnews\u002Fhow-writing-about-schizophrenia-led-hope-recovery\u002F?xid=y_sh\"\u003Emen with schizophrenia\u003C\u002Fa\u003E and those of 100 men without the disease. They then calculated each man&#x2019;s &#x201C;digit ratio,&#x201D; or the length of the index finger compared to that of the ring finger, for each hand.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated: \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.everydayhealth.com\u002Fnews\u002Fways-anger-ruining-your-health\u002F?xid=y_sh\"\u003E\u003Ci\u003E7 Ways Anger Is Ruining Your Health\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EThe results showed that men with schizophrenia had a higher digit ratio on the right hand when compared to the healthy men, meaning they were more likely to have longer right index fingers and shorter ring fingers. Yet, when it came to the left hand, men with schizophrenia had lower digit ratios than those without the disorder.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E&#x201C;Our results suggest that the finger-length ratio has a moderate predictive value for schizophrenia,&#x201D; says study author Taner Oznur, MD, from Gulhane Military Medical Faculty in Ankara, Turkey.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EWhat accounts for this connection? Something that happens during fetal development. Earlier studies have shown that a disturbance of male hormones, such as \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.everydayhealth.com\u002Fdrugs\u002Ftestosterone\u002F?xid=y_sh\"\u003Etestosterone\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, in the womb can influence brain development in a way that increases the risk of schizophrenia and other mental conditions. Hormone levels also influence finger size.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated: \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.everydayhealth.com\u002Fnews\u002Feasy-ways-seniors-can-boost-mental-health-well-being\u002F?xid=y_sh\"\u003E\u003Ci\u003E10 Easy Ways Seniors Can Boost Mental Health and Well-Being\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EDr. Oznur says this hormone imbalance is thought to appear in the third month of pregnancy, but it is difficult to evaluate because of ethical limitations. &#x201C;Therefore, we thought that digit ratio can offer an indirect measure for this evaluation and may reflect early deformities in the brain,&#x201D; he says \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Ch2\u003EFinger Length and Emotional Health Traits\u003C\u002Fh2\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EThe Turkish study isn&#x2019;t the first to look at finger length and how it relates to mental and \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.everydayhealth.com\u002Femotional-health\u002F10-ways-to-boost-emotional-health.aspx?xid=y_sh\"\u003Eemotional health\u003C\u002Fa\u003E. Another small study from the British Psychological Society associated having a shorter index finger and longer ring finger with mental toughness and an aptitude for sports in men. Sixty-seven males who participated in the study had their fingers measured and completed personality and aggression surveys.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E&#x201C;It appears that high prenatal levels of testosterone may result in increased mental toughness, optimism, and hence aptitude toward sport,&#x201D; study author Jim Golby, PhD, head of research in sport and exercise at Teesside University in the United Kingdom said in a statement. &#x201C;This provides tentative support for the conclusion that mental toughness may be partially biologically predetermined.&#x201D;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated: \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.everydayhealth.com\u002Fnews\u002Fmental-health-disorders-may-shorten-life-span\u002F?xid=y_sh\"\u003E\u003Ci\u003EMental Health Disorders May Shorten Life Span\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EIn 2012, researchers measured the digit ratio in 600 young adult volunteers. The results showed that those with smaller digit ratios reported more instances of verbal aggression than those with higher ratios. Furthermore, men in the study had lower digit ratios and higher verbal aggression than the women in the study. A 2015 study published in the journal Personality and Individual Differences found that a smaller finger length ratio in men was associated with kindness &#x2014; defined as being more agreeable and less quarrelsome &#x2014; toward women. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Ch2\u003EDoes Finger Length Really Predict Mental Illness?\u003C\u002Fh2\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ESo how much weight should you place on finger length as a potential \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.everydayhealth.com\u002Fdepression\u002Fmental-iillness-may-be-in-your-genes-1751.aspx?xid=y_sh\"\u003E risk factor for schizophrenia\u003C\u002Fa\u003E or other mental health issues? Not too much, experts say.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E&#x201C;Although I do think this research has potential for understanding the complexity of factors that go into the development of schizophrenia, it is just one potential factor among many and provides another clue for researchers to explore,&#x201D; says Ben Michaelis, PhD, a clinical psychologist and author of Your Next Big Thing: 10 Small Steps to Get Moving and Get Happy. Dr. Michaelis was not involved with the Turkish study.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated: \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.everydayhealth.com\u002Fpictures\u002Fworst-mental-health-treatments-history\u002F?xid=y_sh\"\u003E\u003Ci\u003EThe 10 Worst Mental Health Treatments in History\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EFurthermore, the schizophrenia study and much of the other research in this area is focused solely on men, so little is known about the potential link between finger-length ratios in women and mental health. Oznur also says more research is needed to confirm &#x2014; or disprove &#x2014; the findings.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003EThis article originally appeared on EverydayHealth.com: Health\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003EBy Ashley Welch, \u003Ca To Lose Weight? Stock Up On Avocados And These Four Other Fatty Foods","summary":"If you really want to get in shape, let go of low fat foods and eat these 5 fatty foods instead.","body":"\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002Fbf8dd63fdf51c8054ef46c6a33bed8c711f94c5e.jpg\" alt=\"Want To Lose Weight? Stock Up On Avocados And These Four Other Fatty Foods\" width=\"540\" height=\"270\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Ci\u003EConventional diet advice tells us that if we want to lose weight, we need to eat less fat. The problem? The conventional advice is completely wrong. If you really want to get in shape, let go of &#x201C;low fat&#x201D; foods and eat these 5 fatty foods instead. \u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Ci\u003E(Photo: Getty Images)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EConventional diet advice tells us that if we want to lose weight, we need to eat less fat. The problem? The conventional advice is completely wrong. If you really want to get in shape, let go of &#x201C;low fat&#x201D; foods and eat these 5 fatty foods instead.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Ch2\u003E1. Grass-Fed Butter \u003C\u002Fh2\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EIt may seem counterintuitive at first to make fats the core of the Bulletproof Diet, but given how much your body needs them, it makes sense. Eating a lot of healthy fats is actually much better for you than eating high amounts of almost any other type of food. One of the best ways to get more fat in your diet is to add grass-fed butter to your meals. Butter from grass-fed animals is high in fat-soluble vitamins, antioxidants, healthy fats, and vitamins A, E, D, and K. Grain feeding causes a massive drop in all the beneficial compounds in butter, introduces new toxins, and raises omega-6 levels. It&#x2019;s crucial to choose grass-fed butter every time in order to optimize the health benefits that butter offers.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated\u003Ci\u003E:&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.askmen.com\u002Fvideo\u002Fthrive\u002Fmindful-eating.html\"\u003E\u003Ci\u003ELooking To Get In Better Shape This Summer? Try Mindful Eating \u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Ch2\u003E2. Avocados \u003C\u002Fh2\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EAvocados are a plant source of monounsaturated fat that are easy to make into a delicious and quick meal. Technically the avocado is a fruit, but its nutrient content makes it far more similar to a vegetable. You can eat them raw, mash them up with a small amount of MCT oil and salt, or put them on top of pastured fried eggs. They are one of the most versatile Bulletproof foods you can eat. Just don&#x2019;t cook them!\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated:\u003Ci\u003E&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.askmen.com\u002Fnews\u002Fsports\u002Fhow-a-glass-of-resveratrol-rich-red-wine-can-help-weight-loss.html\"\u003E\u003Ci\u003EHow A Glass Of Resveratrol-Rich Red Wine Can Help Weight Loss\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Ch2\u003E3. Grass-Fed Animal Fat \u003C\u002Fh2\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EGrass-fed animal fat includes bone marrow, tallow, and lard but does not include poultry fat. These Bulletproof-approved fats are high in nutrients, essential fatty acids, protein, minerals, antioxidants, and fat-soluble nutrients that are hard to get elsewhere. These are the most Bulletproof sources of fats on earth and can be added to stocks to create creamy, flavorful soups and stews.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated:&#xA0;\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.askmen.com\u002Fnews\u002Fsports\u002Ffitness-branded-snacks-make-people-eat-more-exercise-less.html\"\u003E\u003Ci\u003EFitness Branded Foods Cause Some People To Eat More, Exercise Less\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Ch2\u003E4. Coconut\u002FMCT Oil \u003C\u002Fh2\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EIn order to optimize the weight loss benefits of eating fat you have to make sure you are consuming the right kinds of fat. The most stable fats are saturated, while the unstable, easily oxidized, and therefore inflammatory fats are polyunsaturated fats. Canola, corn, cottonseed, peanut, safflower, soybean, and sunflower oils are all polyunsaturated. So what oil actually improves your health and aids in weight loss? Virgin coconut oil. This oil has more saturated fat than almost any other food, making it a good choice for cooking because it&#x2019;s so stable. You can also add it to your coffee in the morning in order to boost brain function, increase ketone formation, and assist in fat loss.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated\u003Ci\u003E:&#xA0;\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.askmen.com\u002Fsports\u002Fbodybuilding\u002Fmuscle-growth-hacks.html\"\u003EDave Asprey&#x2019;s 6 Best Muscle Growth Hacks\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Ch2\u003E5. Pastured Eggs \u003C\u002Fh2\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EExcept for potassium and some amino acids, most of the nutrients in eggs are in the yolks, which are extremely high in micronutrients. This means egg-white omelets are not Bulletproof! Just like butter, egg yolks lose most of their nutritional benefits when they come from an animal that was fed antibiotics and GMO corn and soy, which is the diet of essentially all chicken you&#x2019;ll find in supermarkets. Pastured egg yolks have a deep-golden color from the vitamin A and antioxidants, while grain-fed eggs look like regular grain-fed butter &#x2014; pale and watery. If you want to use eggs to help you lose weight you must make sure they are pastured eggs.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EI know the idea of eating more fat to lose weight can be tough to swallow. After all, we&#x2019;ve been taught our whole lives that fats are the enemy. Give these diet tricks a try though and watch the pounds fly off. Then you&#x2019;ll see with your own eyes the secret to getting skinny: eat more fat.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003EDave Asprey is a Silicon Valley tech entrepreneur who spent 15 years and $300,000 to hack his own biology, losing 100 pounds, upgrading his IQ, and lowering his biological age. Tricks To Tell If Someones Lying To You","summary":"Flag a phony with these simple, sneaky strategies.","body":"\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002Fcf37085125827a637d6900a43087dad3b715f942.jpg\" alt=\"3 Tricks To Tell If Someone&#x2019;s Lying To You\" width=\"540\" height=\"342\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003E\u003Cb\u003EFlag a phony with these simple, sneaky strategies \u003C\u002Fb\u003E(Image from Thinkstock)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EWish you had a lie detector to call B.S. on your bluffing buddies or weasely coworkers? Pay closer attention to key details.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EWhether they&#x2019;re telling tiny fibs or tall tales, all liars give off a few red flags, says nonverbal communications consultant Marc Salem, the author of \u003Ci\u003EThe Six Keys to Unlock and Empower Your Mind\u003C\u002Fi\u003E.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EIt&#x2019;s your job to spot those sketchy signs. Here&#x2019;s what to look for the next time you suspect someone&#x2019;s trying to pull a fast one on you.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E(For more clever tricks and super useful advice, check out \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.menshealthbettermanproject.com\u002FmenshealthBetterManProject\u002Findex?cid=BWO_mh.com_html_hp_betterman&amp;keycode=253103\"\u003EThe Better Man Project\u003C\u002Fa\u003E. It&#x2019;s chock full of tips to help you lose fat fast, have hotter sex, and live a kick-ass life!)\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003EListen for Inconsistencies\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Cbr\u003EPay close attention to the way your perpetrator is talking to you and compare it to other conversations you&#x2019;ve had with him. If he&#x2019;s speaking a lot faster or slower than usual, or skipping contractions a la Bill Clinton&#x2014;&#x201C;I \u003Ci\u003Edid not\u003C\u002Fi\u003E have sexual relations with that woman!&#x201D;&#x2014;those are two common slip-ups, Salem says.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ELiars rehearse and put more thought into what they&#x2019;re saying because that&#x2019;s what they think a truth teller would do, says Salem. It&#x2019;s a combination of bad acting and over-selling. Even a good liar has to consciously try to act natural when he knows what he&#x2019;s saying isn&#x2019;t true.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated:\u003C\u002Fb\u003E \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.menshealth.com\u002Fbest-life\u002F10-lies-you-hear-every-day?cm_mmc=Yahoo-_-3_Tricks_To_Tell-_-Entry-_-10_Lies_You_Hear_Daily\"\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Ci\u003EThe 10 Lies You Hear Every Day \u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003EWatch for Weird Body Language\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Cbr\u003EStudy the suspect&#x2019;s body language and see if you can spot the dead giveaways: Is he rubbing his nose or crossing his arms? Is she covering her mouth? If the person doesn&#x2019;t usually exhibit these kinds of behaviors, they could be reasons to dig deeper, says Salem.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EAnd be wary of excessive eye contact: &#x201C;I never trust anyone who stares at me directly in the eyes,&#x201D; Salem says.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EDo you ever catch yourself thinking about how much you blink, and suddenly you&#x2019;re doing it way more than usual? Liars feel a similar effect when they hone in on how their bodies should be during a regular conversation. They might think too much about trying to look relaxed and end up doing something noticeably unnatural&#x2014;like shooting you the death stare for a minute straight.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERope in Your Friends\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Cbr\u003EIf you walk away from a shady conversation and your friends bore witness, ask two of them if they think the suspect was telling the truth. People are more accurate at discerning truth from lies when they&#x2019;re in a group of at least three people, according to research published in \u003Ci\u003EProceedings of the National Academy of Sciences\u003C\u002Fi\u003E. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EWhy it works: There&#x2019;s strength in numbers when it comes to calling out B.S., suggest study authors Nicholas Epley and Nadav Klein. Bouncing ideas and observations off of other people helps you make smarter judgment calls and examine the lie from different perspectives. \u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003EBy Jada Can you answer a few questions for me?&#x201D;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated:&#xA0;\u003Cb\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Ci\u003E\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fthemighty.com\u002F2015\u002F04\u002Fa-man-called-my-son-retarded-one-stranger-wouldnt-stand-for-it?utm_source=yahoo.com&amp;utm_medium=referral&amp;utm_campaign=yahoo_links&amp;utm_content=Called_Son_Retarted\"\u003EA Man Called My Son &#x2018;Retarded.&#x2019; One Stranger Wouldn&#x2019;t Stand for It.\u003C\u002Fa\u003E&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EOf course I can. Sincere questions deserve sincere answers. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EBut what I cannot and will not accept are the accusations, the demands to know what&#x2019;s &#x201C;wrong&#x201D; with me or even the well-intentioned, but unsolicited &#x201C;sympathy.&#x201D; \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ETwelve years ago, I was a high school senior looking forward to a bright future. Just a few months earlier, at age 16, a doctor had diagnosed me with extremely mild cerebral palsy. Many people with cerebral palsy need varying amounts of assistance with walking, talking and other things we take for granted. My case is so mild I don&#x2019;t need any accommodations, besides maybe a little grace from my P.E. teachers when I couldn&#x2019;t quite keep up with my classmates. The actual diagnosis didn&#x2019;t really affect my life; My parents and I were just glad to finally have an explanation for why I lacked gross-motor skills, tended to be hyper-flexible (even though that was a perk in dance and cheerleading!) or why my hands sometimes got the shakes. The diagnosis did not change my plans to go to college in the fall or to become a teacher, nor did it discourage me from playing tennis, taking dance lessons or working my part-time job at a department store. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated:&#xA0;\u003Cb\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fthemighty.com\u002F2014\u002F12\u002Fto-the-woman-who-asked-to-take-a-closer-look-at-my-daughter-with-down-syndrome?utm_source=yahoo.com&amp;utm_medium=referral&amp;utm_campaign=yahoo_links&amp;utm_content=Daughter_with_Down_Syndrome\"\u003E\u003Ci\u003ETo the Woman Who Asked to Take a Closer Look at My Daughter With Down Syndrome\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EIt was at that department store the following encounter took place: I was ringing up a purchase when I heard the sharp command, &#x201C;Stop shaking!&#x201D;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EI looked up to see a man, probably a few years older than my own father, staring down at me in disgust.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E&#x201C;How much coffee have you had today?!&#x201D; he demanded. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EI was 17, and I was supposed to be polite to customers even when they were rude, right? \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E&#x201C;Um, none?&#x201D; I answered. (To this day, I don&#x2019;t even like coffee!) \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E&#x201C;Well, what are you so nervous about?!&#x201D;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EAgain, all I could reply was, &#x201C;Nothing.&#x201D; \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E&#x201C;What&#x2019;s wrong with you?!&#x201D;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EBy now, my heart was starting to race (making the shakes worse, of course), but it wasn&#x2019;t because of fear. I was angry. How were my slightly-shaky hands affecting this guy? What right did he, a complete stranger, have to know about my coffee habits or any other area of my life? Why should I have to justify myself to him? \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated:&#xA0;\u003Cb\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fthemighty.com\u002F2015\u002F01\u002Fthe-odd-thing-about-this-picture-taught-me-a-lesson-we-all-need-to-learn2?utm_source=yahoo.com&amp;utm_medium=referral&amp;utm_campaign=yahoo_links&amp;utm_content=Picture_Taught_Lesson\"\u003E\u003Ci\u003EThe Odd Thing About This Picture Taught Me a Lesson We All Need to Learn\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EI looked up at him. &#x201C;Nothing is wrong with me. Would you like the receipt with you, or in the bag?&#x201D;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ENothing was wrong with me. To this day, nothing is &#x201C;wrong&#x201D; with me. I hold a master&#x2019;s degree and have my dream career. I run and lift weights to stay healthy. I help out with youth group at my church and love to read. I also happen to have mild cerebral palsy. Strengthens Stroke and Heart Attack Warnings on Most NSAIDs","summary":"Lots of us pop pain relievers like ibuprofen as needed, thinking theyre virtually harmless  but thats really not the case, according to new word from the FDA.","body":"\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003E\u003Cb\u003EYou can find many NSAIDs like ibuprofen and naproxen over the counter as products such as Motrin and Aleve.\u003C\u002Fb\u003E (Video: Yahoo Health)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003ELots of us pop pain relievers like ibuprofen as needed, thinking they&#x2019;re virtually harmless &#x2014; but that&#x2019;s really not the case, according to \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.fda.gov\u002FForConsumers\u002FConsumerUpdates\u002Fucm453610.htm?source=govdelivery&amp;utm_medium=email&amp;utm_source=govdelivery\"\u003Enew word\u003C\u002Fa\u003E from the FDA. On Thursday, the agency announced plans to beef up existing heart attack and stroke warnings for both over-the-counter and prescription nonsteroidal anti-inflammatory drugs (NSAIDs).\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003ENSAIDs are used to treat everything from occasional aches and pains to chronic conditions like rheumatoid arthritis and gout. You can find many NSAIDs like ibuprofen and naproxen over the counter as products such as Motrin and Aleve.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EThe FDA wants to issue a big reminder that from the first weeks you begin using an NSAID, there&#x2019;s an increased chance of heart attack and stroke. These risks apply to everyone, whether you&#x2019;re already prone to other cardiovascular events or not.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EAspirin, while an NSAID, was not included in the new FDA warnings.\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003EWhy now?\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EThere are probably two reasons we&#x2019;re seeing a stronger FDA advisory now, says Prashant Vaishnava, a cardiologist at Mount Sinai Heart of the Mount Sinai Hospital and an assistant professor of medicine of Icahn School of Medicine at Mount Sinai.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E&#x201C;We&#x2019;re better understanding the mechanism behind why there&#x2019;s an increased risk of cardiovascular events, and that&#x2019;s likely the inhibition of the COX-2 enzymes,&#x201D; Vaishnava tells Yahoo Health. &#x201C;The other reason is there&#x2019;s a new focus on over-the-counter medications, which lots of people take without being fully aware of the risk.&#x201D;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EThe risks are widespread &#x2014; something we&#x2019;re finding out more and more with research. Take for example a \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwell.blogs.nytimes.com\u002F2013\u002F06\u002F17\u002Fthe-heart-perils-of-pain-relievers\u002F\"\u003Ehuge Lancet analysis\u003C\u002Fa\u003E of more than 600 studies and 350,000 people, which showed that significant doses of these medications daily can increase your risk of a cardiovascular event by up to a third.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EAnd a \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.bmj.com\u002Fcontent\u002F342\u002Fbmj.c7086\"\u003Esurvey of evidence published in the BMJ\u003C\u002Fa\u003E in 2011 concluded there was little data to suggest that any NSAIDs were notably safe for the heart (although naproxen did seem to be the least harmful, in cardiovascular terms).\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003EWhat&#x2019;s next, and how to take NSAIDs safely\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EWhile there&#x2019;s already a note about heart attack and stroke risk on current NSAID labels, the FDA will request that manufacturers begin to roll out more-detailed instructions on the potential for complications. Expect to see additional warnings on labels and within the &#x201C;Drug Facts.&#x201D;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EVaishnava says it&#x2019;s always smart to consult with your doctor before taking a new medication &#x2014; even an over-the-counter pill like ibuprofen or naproxen. &#x201C;Anyone with a history of coronary artery disease, heart attack, or bypass surgery especially shouldn&#x2019;t take NSAIDs,&#x201D; he says. &#x201C;There&#x2019;s good data showing it&#x2019;s better to avoid these, and I always tell my patients to try acetaminophen [Tylenol] first if there is no contraindication to it.&#x201D;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EThat said, acetaminophen has its own set of limitations. Vaishnava says its anti-inflammatory properties are limited, it can lead to liver toxicity at high doses, and it doesn&#x2019;t always ease everyone&#x2019;s pain symptoms. &#x201C;Decisions about the use of OTC medications should be individualized,&#x201D; he says.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EIf you&#x2019;re not 100 percent sure what&#x2019;s in a pain reliever or medication, read the label carefully. Don&#x2019;t take multiple medications specifying the same active ingredient. &#x201C;It&#x2019;s also important to realize you may be taking an NSAID and not realize it, especially if you&#x2019;re taking a combination pill,&#x201D; like a multisymptom cold-relief medication, Vaishnava says.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EFinally, be mindful of use. If an over-the-counter pain reliever isn&#x2019;t actually working to improve your symptoms, stop taking it. And if you have symptoms of a heart issue while taking NSAIDs, like chest pain, difficulty breathing, or weakness in a part of the body, seek medical attention immediately.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E
