Confirms What We Knew All Along: Nurses Are Key to Hospital Success","summary":"Have you thanked a nurse lately? Youll want to after reading this.","body":"\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E \n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F53337bc822bb693ebef56c02aef29e521f49b706.jpg\" alt=\"Study Confirms What We Knew All Along: Nurses Are Key to Hospital Success\" width=\"540\" height=\"361\"\u003E \n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003E\u003Cb\u003EHave you thanked a nurse lately? You&#x2019;ll want to after reading this. \u003C\u002Fb\u003E(David Leahy\u002FJuice Images\u002FCorbis)&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EIf you&#x2019;ve ever had a loved one in the hospital, you know how important nurses are. \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.biomedcentral.com\u002Fcontent\u002Fpdf\u002F1472-6963-11-319.pdf\"\u003EStudies show\u003C\u002Fa\u003E that the amount of time that nurses spend with patients is related to fewer errors. And according to a \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov\u002Fpubmed\u002F26131607\"\u003Enew study\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, investing in nursing is key to patient outcomes, including the risk of dying while in the hospital.\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EThe study&#x2019;s researchers, a team from the University of Pennsylvania, wanted to understand why certain hospitals have better outcomes than others. Specifically, the UPenn team was trying to explain why hospitals in the \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fhealthy.kaiserpermanente.org\u002Fhtml\u002Fkaiser\u002Findex.shtml\"\u003EKaiser Permanente\u003C\u002Fa\u003E health care system &#x2014; an integrated health network in eight states that includes hospitals, insurance, and doctors&#x2019; offices all in one system &#x2014; have such efficient and high-quality care.&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EOther organizations have tried to mimic Kaiser Permanente&#x2019;s organizational structure in order to improve care, but with mixed results. The researchers thought there might be a different X factor that could explain Kaiser&#x2019;s success: nurses.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EIn order to find out, the study looked at more than 550 hospitals in California, New Jersey, Pennsylvania, and Florida, including 25 California-based Kaiser Permanente hospitals and 56 Magnet hospitals. Magnet hospitals are recognized by the American Nurses Credentialing Center for being good workplaces for nurses.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E \n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"500\" height=\"363\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fdiminuendo\u002F1.0\u002Foriginal\u002Fd9a934b2b50bd8e5473057b62c711b55eb5e8452.gif\"\u003E \n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003EScrubs\u003Ci\u003E was right all along. \u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Ci\u003E(Image: Fox\u002FScrubs)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003ENurses in each hospital answered surveys about their work environment, level of education, job satisfaction, and the number of patients visited during a typical shift. The researchers also pulled data on patient mortality.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E&#x201C;It turns out that, by and large, nursing differences accounted for much of the mortality difference that we saw in Kaiser Permanente hospitals,&#x201D; says study author \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.nursing.upenn.edu\u002Ffaculty\u002Fprofile.asp?pid=2533\"\u003EMatthew McHugh\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, PhD, RN, a professor at the \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.nursing.upenn.edu\u002FPages\u002Fdefault.aspx\"\u003EUniversity of Pennsylvania School of Nursing.\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EThe results were clear: The odds of dying were about 20 percent lower in Kaiser Permanente&#xA0;and Magnet hospitals, and differences in nursing accounted for &#x201C;a sizeable portion of the advantage,&#x201D; according to the study. The analysis adjusted for factors such as hospital size and the severity of patients&#x2019; conditions.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E&#x201C;It turns out that these differences we see in nursing, in terms of work environment, staffing levels, investment in nursing around a highly educated workforce, those things translate into better outcomes,&#x201D; McHugh tells Yahoo Health. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EThere were a few specific factors that made Kaiser and Magnet hospitals stand out from the rest, McHugh explains:\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E1. Better work environments\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EHappier nurses mean healthier patients, research shows. &#x201C;We find that places where nurses have a good experience working are places where nurses are better able to do their jobs. They&#x2019;re more autonomous, they&#x2019;re supported by management, and they&#x2019;re integrated into hospital decision-making,&#x201D; McHugh says.\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EEmpowered nurses have better relationships with physicians, &#x201C;so when they say &#x2018;something isn&#x2019;t right,&#x2019; they&#x2019;ll be taken seriously,&#x201D; McHugh adds. And patients can receive faster and more efficient care when nurses are authorized to make decisions such as when to remove a catheter, for example.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EIn fact, a \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.researchgate.net\u002Fprofile\u002FHeather_Laschinger\u002Fpublication\u002F262581884_The_influence_of_nursing_unit_empowerment_and_social_capital_on_unit_effectiveness_and_nurse_perceptions_of_patient_care_quality\u002Flinks\u002F5485dcb70cf289302e28747c.pdf\"\u003Estudy\u003C\u002Fa\u003E published last year in the \u003Ci\u003EJournal of Nursing Administration\u003C\u002Fi\u003E found that empowered nursing units are more effective and report better patient care compared to units with less authority.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003ETangible changes matter, too. In response to the nurse shortage in the early 2000s, Kaiser Permanente made a deliberate, research-based effort to invest in nursing, says \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fnursingpathways.kp.org\u002Fnational\u002Fhome\u002Fmessages\u002Findex.html\"\u003EMarilyn Chow\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, PhD, RN, Vice President of National Patient Care Services and Innovation for Kaiser Permanente.&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EA \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov\u002Fpmc\u002Farticles\u002FPMC3037121\u002F\"\u003Estudy\u003C\u002Fa\u003E of Kaiser hospitals conducted in 2005 and 2006 found that nurses spent more than 35 percent of their time on documentation. Starting in 2005, the system switched to electronic medical records, which helped streamline paperwork. They also observed that nurses spent a lot of time hunting and gathering equipment and information &#x2014; checking to see if a medication was ready, for instance. In response, Kaiser Permanente rearranged the work environment to make things more convenient. (Nurses now receive a notification when meds are ready for pickup.)\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E&#x201C;We wanted to make sure that we were a place that nurses wanted to work,&#x201D; Chow tells Yahoo Health. &#x201C;If you have nurses who are happy and joyful at their work, they will definitely pass that on and be caring and compassionate.&#x201D;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated: \u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.yahoo.com\u002Fhealth\u002Fdoctor-bullying-and-ward-rage-the-challenges-119959215917.html\"\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Ci\u003EDoctor Bullying and&#xA0;&#x2018;Ward Rage&#x2019;: The Challenges Faced by Nurses Every Day\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E2. More nurses with Bachelor&#x2019;s degrees\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EThe role of the nurse is \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fshare.kaiserpermanente.org\u002Farticle\u002Fkaiser-permanentes-marilyn-chow-interviewed-about-changing-role-of-nurses\u002F\"\u003Emuch more complex\u003C\u002Fa\u003E than it used to be, Chow explains. &#x201C;The role is not only surveillance, but facilitating and coordinating the care, and not just for one patient, but for four to five patients &#x2026; there are so many things to take care of,&#x201D; she says. Patients also arrive sicker and leave the hospital earlier, Chow and McHugh say, which puts an extra demand on nurses to coordinate care and teach patients and family members what to do when they arrive home. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E&#x201C;Hospitals are very complex, and integrating all of that information requires a certain set of skills and requires you have a pool of knowledge within the overall nursing staff,&#x201D; McHugh explains. He adds that the study observed a wide variation in nurse education from hospital to hospital, and that variation was associated with adverse events.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated: \u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.yahoo.com\u002Fhealth\u002Fthe-video-above-is-titled-love-our-nurses-and-117118143767.html\"\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Ci\u003EWatch This Girl, Paralyzed for 11 Days, Surprise Her Nurse By Walking\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E3. More nurses, period\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EKaiser Permanente hospitals have a 4-to-1 patient-to-nurse ratio, on average, compared to 5-to-1 in non-Magnet hospitals, the UPenn study found.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EHaving more nurses ensures that there are enough eyes in rooms monitoring patients. It also means that nurses have sufficient time to follow up with patients and communicate effectively. &#x201C;Nurses are at the bedside and are working with all the other providers. They&#x2019;re the essential person for monitoring patient condition, and if something bad does happen, intervening and mobilizing the intervention response,&#x201D; McHugh says.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E \n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"500\" height=\"376\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fdiminuendo\u002F1.0\u002Foriginal\u002Fb43ab18ee18fbb7e7be1d3e8f830c2a897f7d7b9.gif\"\u003E \n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003E\u003Cb\u003EYou tell it, Carla.\u003C\u002Fb\u003E (Image: Fox\u002FScrubs)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERead This Next:\u003C\u002Fb\u003E \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.yahoo.com\u002Fhealth\u002Fsymptom-checker-websites-miss-millions-of-123664133232.html\"\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Ci\u003ESymptom Checker Websites Miss Millions of Emergencies, Study Warms\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003ELet&#x2019;s keep in touch! 10 Cities Where People Dont Look Their Age","summary":"You know how some people just seem to defy the hands of time? If you live in one of Americas youngest-looking cities, theres a chance youre one of those people. Is your city on the list?","body":"\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002Fa153d5a2f17c4541149ea71d3ccf1e57cb43c6a5.jpg\" alt=\"Top 10 Cities Where People Don&#x2019;t Look Their Age\" width=\"540\" height=\"271\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003E\u003Cb\u003EIs your hometown on the list?\u003C\u002Fb\u003E (Photo: Getty Images)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EYou know how some people just seem to defy the hands of time? If you live in one of America&#x2019;s youngest-looking cities, there&#x2019;s a chance you&#x2019;re one of those people.\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EThe survey considered&#xA0;lifestyle factors that affect skin aging, like sun exposure, stress, pollution, average sleep logged, fitness levels, and the prevalence of smoking and alcohol consumption &#x2014; looking at American cities with populations over 300,000. &#x201C;We analyzed a handful of data points that doctors say matter most if you want to keep people guessing your age for decades to come,&#x201D; says Tom Seery, founder and CEO of \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.realself.com\"\u003ERealSelf.com\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, which \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Ftrends.realself.com\u002F2015\u002F07\u002F08\u002Ftop-10-cities-staying-young\"\u003Econducted the survey\u003C\u002Fa\u003E.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"505\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002Ff984deef79975ed84f69fed2be658e96967fbedd.jpg\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003E(Graphic: Courtesy of Real Self)&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ETopping the list of young-looking cities is Minneapolis, Minnesota, where the locals are not only fitter than average, but also get plenty of sleep. Seattle came in second, thanks mostly to the overcast skies that keep sun exposure very low, while San Francisco, clocked in at third place thanks to its active residents who also catch an ample amount of shut-eye. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ESalt Lake City has the lowest smoking rate in the U.S., along with low amounts of stress and drinking, bringing it to fourth. Sunny cities like Honolulu and San Diego still cracked the top 10 in spite of all those ultraviolet rays; both boast healthy, slower-paced lifestyles that are antidotes to aging. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EMeanwhile, sun-drenched locales accompanied by heavy aging factors sunk some cities. At the bottom of the list is Riverside, CA, which has skyrocketing stress levels (perhaps&#xA0;due to one of the highest unemployment rates in the country), while the smoky and boozy late night culture of Las Vegas has it sitting second-to-last.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated: \u003Ci\u003E\u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.yahoo.com\u002Fhealth\u002Fwhy-skin-wrinkles-more-in-certain-areas-123583834227.html\"\u003EWhy Skin Wrinkles More In Certain Areas\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EHigher rates of obesity, smoking, drinking, and poor sleep habits all plummeted cities like New Orleans, Detroit, Albuquerque and Oklahoma City to the bottom of the list. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EExperts say that while skincare products can certainly help skin look younger, it&#x2019;s our daily lifestyles that influence the way we look the most. &#x201C;Age management has to do with managing your stress levels and learning to say &#x2018;no&#x2019; when you&#x2019;re overwhelmed, taking care of yourself and making sure you exercise regularly,&#x201D; says Montclair, New Jersey dermatologist, \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.imagedermatology.com\u002F\"\u003EJeanine B. Downie, MD\u003C\u002Fa\u003E. &#x201C;As we get older, we need to sleep more to help our bodies recover,&#x201D; she adds.\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EIf you live in a city with high aging factors, Dr. Downie says staying active is one of the best ways to negate the effects. &#x201C;As you get older, regularly exercising more intensely for shorter bursts of time is one of the best ways to stay fit and young as we age in our stressful society,&#x201D; advises Downie. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EKnown as interval training, research has shown that these shorter 15 to 20 minute bursts of higher intensity exercise (in comparison to longer light or moderate workouts) not only oxygenate the body to help relieve stress, but also offer a variety of anti-aging benefits, including burning more fat and moving sugar out of the bloodstream for healthier blood sugar levels. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERead This Next: \u003Ci\u003E\u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.yahoo.com\u002Fhealth\u002Fthe-part-of-your-face-you-absolutely-need-to-122973275813.html\"\u003EThe Part of your Face You Absolutely Need to Protect from the Sun&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003ELet&#x2019;s keep in touch!
